# <a name="hlsl-errors-and-warnings"></a><span data-ttu-id="52a9f-103">Ошибки и предупреждения HLSL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52a9f-103">HLSL errors and warnings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52a9f-104">Коды ошибок и предупреждений, которые может вернуть шейдер.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52a9f-104">Error and warning codes that a shader can return.</span></span>

| <span id="ERR_COMMENTEOF"></span><span id="err_commenteof"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="52a9f-107"><dt>**Ошибка \_ КОММЕНТЕОФ**</dt> <dt>1001</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52a9f-107"><dt>**ERR\_COMMENTEOF**</dt> <dt>1001</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                                 | <span data-ttu-id="52a9f-108">Комментарий остается после конца файла.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52a9f-108">A comment continues past the end of file.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| <span id="ERR_HEXTRUNCATED"></span><span id="err_hextruncated"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="52a9f-109"><dt>**Ошибка \_ ХЕКСТРУНКАТЕД**</dt> <dt>1002</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52a9f-109"><dt>**ERR\_HEXTRUNCATED**</dt> <dt>1002</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                           | <span data-ttu-id="52a9f-110">Шестнадцатеричное значение было усечено до 32 бит.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52a9f-110">A hex value was truncated to 32 bits.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span id="ERR_OCTTRUNCATED"></span><span id="err_octtruncated"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="52a9f-111"><dt>**Ошибка \_ ОКТТРУНКАТЕД**</dt> <dt>1003</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52a9f-111"><dt>**ERR\_OCTTRUNCATED**</dt> <dt>1003</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                           | <span data-ttu-id="52a9f-112">Восьмеричное значение было усечено до 32 бит.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52a9f-112">An octal value was truncated to 32 bits.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
